<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:специальный.html>специа́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">speciálʹnyj</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:специфичный.html>специфи́чный</a> (31184)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">spezif(isch)</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́чный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:специфика.html>специ́фика</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">specífika</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́чный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:печь.html>печь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pečʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fail, come a cropper</li></ol>

***спешить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спешить.html>спеши́ть</a> (1190)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">спѣшити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spěšiti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*spěšiti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hurry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*spěxъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">haste</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*spěti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to advance, ripen, hurry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-xъ</i>. Equivalently from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">спех</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spex</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спеть.html>спеть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spetʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спешить.html>спеши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spešítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заспешить.html>заспеши́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поспешить.html>поспеши́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to hurry, to hasten, to make haste, to be in a hurry</li>
<li>to be fast <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">said of clocks, watches</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<ol><li>to cause to dismount <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">from a horse or bicycle, get out of a vehicle</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***спешка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спешка.html>спе́шка</a> (11605)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спешить.html>спеши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spešítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спешка.html>спе́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spéška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спешка.html>спе́шки</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hurry, haste
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куда.html>куда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>така́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спешка.html>спе́шка</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kudá takája <b>spéška</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Why the rush?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спешка.html>спе́шке</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>spéške</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in a hurry</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>без</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спешка.html>спе́шки</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bez <b>spéški</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">without rush</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спидометр.html>спидо́метр</a> (22985)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">speedometer</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спидометр.html>спидо́метр</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spidómetr</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спидометр.html>спидо́метра</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спидометр.html>спидо́метры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спидометр.html>спидо́метров</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>speedometer (a device that measures, and indicates the current speed of a vehicle)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">ана́логовый <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спидометр.html>спидо́метр</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">análogovyj <b>spidómetr</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">analog speedometer</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:барабанный.html>бараба́нный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спидометр.html>спидо́метр</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">barabánnyj <b>spidómetr</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">revolving drum speedometer</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">ле́нточный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спидометр.html>спидо́метр</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">léntočnyj <b>spidómetr</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">ribbon speedometer</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">стре́лочный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спидометр.html>спидо́метр</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stréločnyj <b>spidómetr</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">needle speedometer</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:цифровой.html>цифрово́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спидометр.html>спидо́метр</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">cifrovój <b>spidómetr</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">digital speedometer</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спикер.html>спи́кер</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spíker</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спикер.html>спи́кера</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спикер.html>спи́керы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спикер.html>спи́керов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>speaker (<i>the chair or presiding officer</i>)</li>
<li>loudspeaker (<i>transducer</i>)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">говоритель</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">govoritelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***спина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спина́</a> (303)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*spey-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sharp point</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">spine</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">spike</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спина́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spiná</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спины́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спи́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спи́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> back</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спинка.html>спи́нка</a> (3332)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спина́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spiná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спинка.html>спи́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spínka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спинка.html>спи́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спинка.html>спи́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спинка.html>спи́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спина.html>спина́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spiná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li>back <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of a chair, couch or other furniture, of a dress or a shirt, of a tool, of an animal, or as a cut of meat</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>; headboard; backrest</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спираль.html>спира́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spirálʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спираль.html>спира́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спираль.html>спира́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спираль.html>спира́лей</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спираль.html>спира́ль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spirálʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***спирт.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спирт.html>спирт</a> (2816)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">spirit</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">spīritus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спирт.html>спирт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spirt</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спирт.html>спи́рта</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спирт.html>спирты́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спирт.html>спирто́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>alcohol, spirits
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:технический.html>техни́ческий</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спирт.html>спирт</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">texníčeskij <b>spirt</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">denatured alcohol</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">гидро́лизный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:спирт.html>спирт</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gidróliznyj <b>spirt</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">cellulosic ethanol</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:спиртной.html>спиртно́й</a> (6795)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спирт.html>спирт</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spirt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
<ol><li>alcoholic, spirituous

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:списание.html>списа́ние</a> (27942)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:списать.html>списа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">spisátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:списание.html>списа́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">spisánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:списание.html>списа́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:списание.html>списа́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:списание.html>списа́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>write-off
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:списание.html>списа́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:задолженность.html>задо́лженности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spisánije</b> zadólžennosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">debt forgiveness</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:списание.html>списа́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:долгий.html>до́лга</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spisánije</b> dólga</i> ― <span class="e-translation">debt relief</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:списание.html>списа́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:счет.html>счёта</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>spisánije</b> so sčóta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">charge-off</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
